## Last shipped session

**#889 EVENT WINDOWS ‚Äî PER-DAY VOLUME LEVELS (per-DATE schedule within one reduced_volume window) (2026-06-29; branch `claude/issue-889-7ja7tu`; PR [#989](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/989); issue [#889](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/issues/889) ‚Äî go-live blocker, Andy-directed detour off the #884 thread).** A `reduced_volume` window scaled **every** covered day by its single `volume_pct`, so a multi-day trip with one light day over-reduced the rest. Fixed in two commits: **(1) single-day ergonomics + scope clarity** ‚Äî `end_date` optional on add (blank ‚Üí `end==start`; blank *start* still rejected), the list renders a one-day window as `<date> (1 day)` not `X ‚Üí X`, and the form states the % blankets every covered day; **(2) per-DATE schedule** ‚Äî a `reduced_volume` window now carries `volume_by_date` (each covered day dials independently; **100% = a normal, unreduced day**). **The plan-gen change is tiny because the per-day union mechanics already existed:** the generator already cuts the plan span at window boundaries and resolves each day against the covering segment's `volume_pct`, so a scheduled window **expands into one-day overrides** in `orchestrator._build_event_window_overlay` (full 1.0 days emit nothing; unmapped dates fall back to the window-wide pct) ‚Äî segmentation, the per-week capacity factor, the synthesis overlay, and the Rule #15 log all run **unchanged**; a window with **no** schedule stays one override ‚Üí byte-identical to pre-#889 (regression-tested). **Surface:** `init_db.py` migration (`athlete_event_windows.volume_by_date` TEXT JSON, driver-agnostic like `brought_craft`, NULL = window-wide pct); `athlete_event_windows_repo.py` (`EventWindow.volume_by_date` + load parse, `load_event_window`, `update_event_window_volume_by_date` writer validating date/range/level `0<pct<=1.0`, stored sorted for a stable digest); `orchestrator.py` per-day expansion; `hashing.py` folds `volume_by_date` into `compute_event_windows_hash` (a per-day edit invalidates the overlapping synthesis); `routes/profile.py` + new `templates/profile/event_window_volume_days.html` (strict-CSP-safe per-day editor ‚Äî one percent select per covered date, reached from a "Per-day levels" link on each multi-day reduced_volume row; Rule #15 log). **`no_training` unchanged** ‚Äî per-day is reduced_volume-only (`0<pct<=1.0`); a fully-off day stays its own `no_training` window (it also drops the day from the placement pool, which a per-date 0% wouldn't). **VERIFIED:** full suite (merged with latest `main`) **3660 passed / 30 skipped** (+15 new tests: repo load/validate/write, orchestrator per-day expansion + no-schedule regression, hash sensitivity, route GET/POST, render). **DDL auto-applies on deploy** (public-schema `_PG_MIGRATIONS`; no Neon apply owed). **NEXT: back to the #884 thread ‚Äî slice 4b PR-3** (2C `cluster_gear_toggle_states` un-starve) then slice 4.3.

### Predecessor ‚Äî #884 UNIFIED GEAR/CRAFT MODEL ‚Äî SLICE 4b PR-2: GEAR/TERRAIN CASCADE EXTENSION (2026-06-29; branch `claude/884-gear-toggle-capture-w4nug5`; PR [#983](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/983) ‚Äî auto-merge SQUASH armed; swim stays drill-gating-only). **Two findings ‚Üí two ratified decisions (Andy 2026-06-29, AskUserQuestion):** (1) the gear taxonomy (`ski/snow/climbing/alpine`) DIVERGES from the discipline modality taxonomy (`snow/climb/foot`), so the cascade now derives `target_kind` from the **gear-side** `gear_discipline_aliases` (`discipline_gear_kind`), NOT `modality_groups` ‚Äî bike/paddle coincide ‚Üí byte-identical (pinned by the existing tier tests); dropped the modality `group_kind` param, added `discipline_gear_kind` + `craft_fidelity_rank`; `same_kind` now walks ASCENDING `fidelity_rank` (D-028 ladder classic 0‚Üískate 1‚Üírollerskis 2; bike/paddle all rank 0 ‚Üí prior slug order). **`orchestrator.py`:** new `_q_gear_fidelity_rank`; `discipline_gear_kind` derived in `_gather_feasibility_inputs` (no new query); Rule #15 `_craft_kind_of` log repointed; widened `_CRAFT_ALIAS_GROUP_KINDS`. **Migration `0026`** (10 `craft_terrain_compatibility` rows, `0A-v1.9.2`, reuse existing terrain vocab ‚Äî NO new entries): ski/snow/climbing/alpine gear ‚Üí their disciplines' required terrains, with the **rollerskis‚ÜíTRN-001 dryland carve-out** (own-gear-alternate-terrain PROXY tier). **INTENDED served-output change:** gear now gates ‚Äî own skis + snow ‚Üí EXACT; no skis ‚Üí INDOOR/STRENGTH even with snow; **bike/paddle UNCHANGED**. **`craft_terrain_compatibility` is live-read + family 0A** ‚Üí the new digest invalidates plan caches (correct). **+ TAXONOMY NORMALIZATION (Andy 2026-06-29, directed to land together):** renamed the gear kind **`climbing`‚Üí`climb`** to align with the modality vocab (the only true naming collision; ski/snow/alpine keep their finer gear-family names ‚Äî the single modality `snow` splits into three so snowshoes never proxy for skis). Three pieces (the cumulative option Andy picked): **(1) rename** `climbing`‚Üí`climb` ‚Äî `GEAR_REGISTRY`/`_GEAR_TOGGLE_KINDS`/both cascade sets + **layer0 `0027`** (`gear_discipline_aliases`, idempotent UPDATE ‚Äî new file since the apply loop runs each once by ledger) + **`init_db._PG_MIGRATIONS`** live `athlete_gear` rename (auto-applies on deploy); **(2) retire** the dead modality `group_kind` plumbing ‚Äî removed `_q_modality_group_kind` + `_FeasibilityInputs.group_kind_by_group` (write-only after the gear-side cutover ‚Üí ONE group_kind source); **(3) drop** the unused column ‚Äî **layer0 `0028`** (`modality_groups.group_kind` DROP COLUMN IF EXISTS; no reader ‚Äî 2A pooling keys on group MEMBERSHIP). `0027`+`0028` land in the SAME `layer0-apply` run as `0026` (else climbing briefly degrades to terrain-only). **VERIFIED:** suite **3709 passed / 30 skipped** (+17; only the 3 #217 warnings); ruff clean (the 1 E402 in init_db.py pre-exists HEAD); migrations `0026`+`0027`+`0028` validated on PG16 (apply + idempotent + `validate_layer0` PASS). **4 code + 3 migrations + 5 test files** (over ceiling ‚Äî cohesive changes Andy bundled; most test edits mechanical). **Neon apply OWED** (`layer0-apply`, `0026`+`0027`+`0028` one run). **NEXT: PR-3** (2C `cluster_gear_toggle_states` un-starve ‚Äî needs a `gear_id‚Üítoggle_name` bridge) **then slice 4.3** (redump retiring `craft_discipline_aliases` + equipment strip). **STAY ON THE #884 THREAD** (design-v3 ¬ß15: 4b‚ÜíPR3‚Üí4.3‚Üí5‚Üí6).

`_WELLNESS_SOURCE_PRIORITY` is now only the tiebreak), and `_coalesce(candidates, ranked, pinned)` picks the **hard pin** first (decision 1 ‚Äî if the pinned provider has a value for the metric it wins) else the first ranked source that carries the metric (primary-first per-metric gap-fill). `materialize_canonical_wellness` reads the wellness pin once via `source_preferences_repo.get_source_preferences(db, uid)` (lazy import ‚Äî avoids the `source_preferences_repo ‚Üí canonical_wellness` cycle); the 3A cache row itself natural-misses on its `integration_bundle_hash` (derived from the re-materialized table ‚Äî Layer3A spec ¬ß9.2), so only the downstream L4/3B rows need eviction. **B4's picker route will call this after `set`/`clear`.** **Cache note (benign, one-time):** switching freshest‚Üímost-complete re-coalesces every multi-source day, so the first materialize after deploy shifts the 3A bundle hash once (re-synth on next plan run). **Tests:** `test_canonical_wellness.py` `TestCoalesce` rewritten to most-complete (completeness-beats-priority, gap-fill from a lesser source, priority tiebreak on equal completeness) + new `TestHardPin` (pin wins over a more-complete source; new `tests/test_source_preference_apply.py` (+2: re-materialize-then-evict-layer3a, user-scoped). **3 substantive files** (`canonical_wellness.py`, `source_preference_apply.py`, + the apply test) within ceiling. **No schema/DDL ‚Üí no Neon apply owed** (B1's table is live). **Full suite 3622 passed / 30 skipped** (the 3 Layer3B `evidence_basis` warnings pre-exist, #217). **NEXT ‚Äî B3** (cardio merge + pin: thread the cardio pin into `materialize_canonical_activity`, re-materialize affected clusters on pin change), then **B4** (two-dropdown picker UI ‚Üí `set`/`clear` + the B2/B3 apply helpers; **freshness = gate** (inject only when recent HRV/sleep exists); **posture = strong-lean** (push hard toward de-load on poor recovery, no hard rule). **New `layer4/recovery_guidance.py` `format_recovery_guidance(layer3a_payload) -> list[str]`** (single home so the wording is shared, not copy-pasted): gate `fresh = data_density.recent_hrv_count>0 or recent_sleep_count>0`. **Block A (fresh):** surfaces the previously-hidden 3A fields ‚Äî `recent_trajectory.short_term/medium_term.{direction,reasoning_text}`, **per-discipline** `acwr_status` (was combined-only), and `notable_observations` filtered to `warning`/`data_gap` ‚Äî then the strong-lean directive ("PRIORITIZE recovery ‚Ä¶ pull volume to the lower edge of the band, cut intensity, bias Z1-Z2, unless race-proximity overrides ‚Ä¶ not a hard rule, separate from the calendar deload cadence"). **Block B (no data ‚Äî today's default until Andy re-uploads post-#934):** an explicit "Do not infer a recovery state from absent data ‚Äî plan the normal progression" line. **Rule #15** `[recovery-guidance] fresh=‚Ä¶ short=‚Ä¶ acwr_combined_zone=‚Ä¶ hrv_n=‚Ä¶ sleep_n=‚Ä¶ injected_block=A|B` print. Wired into both `layer4/plan_refresh_t2.py` + `layer4/plan_refresh_t3.py` right after the existing `=== Athlete state (3A) ===` block (`parts.extend(format_recovery_guidance(...))`). **3 substantive files** (`recovery_guidance.py` + the 2 tier files) + **new `tests/test_layer4_plan_refresh_recovery.py` (+6)** (gate both ways; strong-lean directive present on fresh / **absent** on no-data; per-discipline ACWR + reasoning surfaced; observation-category filtering; empty sub-lists omitted; both tiers share the one helper). **No new payload field, no schema/DDL ‚Üí no Neon apply owed, and `plan_refresh_key` inputs are untouched ‚Üí no cache invalidation / forced re-runs.** **Full suite 3588 passed / 30 skipped** (the 3 Layer3B `evidence_basis` warnings pre-exist, #217). **LIVE-VERIFY owed (Andy, gated on data):** after the wellness re-upload ‚Üí 3A digests it ‚Üí a T2/T3 refresh shows `[recovery-guidance] fresh=True` in `/admin/logs` and eases load on a fatigued/overreach day. **NEXT ‚Äî Phase 4 Slice 2:** fold the same helper into PerPhase / RaceWeekBrief / single_session. _(#884 gear/craft PAUSED mid-arc at slice 3b ‚Äî slices 4‚Üí6 remain.)_

### Predecessor ‚Äî #196 Phase 2 Slice 2.3 (repoint the Layer-3A wellness reader)

**INTEGRATIONS / #196 ‚Äî PHASE 2 SLICE 2.3: REPOINT THE LAYER-3A WELLNESS READER AT THE CANONICAL TABLE (2026-06-28; **MERGED ‚Äî PR [#935](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/935), commit `b82d6dc`** [the closing handoff predates the merge and still says "PR not yet opened"]; design `designs/CanonicalDailyWellness_196_Phase2_Design_v1.md`; handoff `handoffs/V5_Implementation_CanonicalDailyWellness_196_Phase2_Slice2_3_2026_06_28_Closing_Handoff_v1.md`).** `layer3a/integration.py:q_layer3A_recent_wellness` no longer runs the inline six-source freshest-non-null coalesce ‚Äî it's now a thin `SELECT ‚Ä¶ FROM canonical_daily_wellness` of the row Slice 2.2 materializes, mapping the TEXT date back to a `date` and **skipping context-only rows** (Garmin readiness/vo2max with no merged device sleep/HRV/resting-HR ‚Äî the old coalesce only emitted days with ‚â•1 device value). The repoint is then **byte-identical** to the retired path. **Tests:** rewrote `TestRecentWellness` to the canonical-read shape; fixed the 3 `TestAssembleBundle` query-count tests (wellness now 1 read, not 6 ‚Üí 12-query bundle); **new `tests/test_wellness_reader_equality.py`** asserts the verbatim-old-reader and new-materialize+read `recent_wellness` lists are identical. **Full suite 3582 passed / 30 skipped.** **OPEN (decide at build):** the optional `/wellness` chart repoint (`routes/wellness.py`) was **deferred**; `coaching.get_wellness_summary` stays out of scope (v1-only).

singletons get a canonical row too (Slice 4 reads uniformly). **Rule #15:** `[cardio-canon] cluster=‚Ä¶ members=‚Ä¶ primary=id‚Ä¶/<provider> score=‚Ä¶ fields={field<-provider,‚Ä¶}`. **3 substantive files** (`init_db.py`, `routes/garmin.py`, `tests/test_garmin_bulk_source.py` ‚Äî `TestCompletenessScore` / `TestRowProvider` / `TestMaterializeCanonical`, **+10**). **Tests:** full suite **3502 passed / 30 skipped**; `'other'`/unknown is a wildcard that never blocks a start+duration/distance-corroborated merge. **No-fork guarantee:** `pg_advisory_xact_lock(196, user_id)` serializes find-or-create so two near-simultaneous webhooks (Wahoo + its Strava auto-forward) can't both open a cluster (txn-scoped; autocommit off ‚Äî `database.py`). **NULL `started_at`** ‚Üí left unclustered (never false-merge; kickoff ¬ß6). **Match rule:** start in window AND loose sport AND no metric clearly disagreeing AND ‚â•1 of duration/distance corroborating ‚Äî so a bare start coincidence (0 distance + unknown duration) never merges; the indoor repro (distance 0 on both) clusters on duration. **Rule #15:** `[cardio-cluster] ‚Ä¶ ‚Üí MATCH/NEW cluster=‚Ä¶` logs inputs + decision + candidate count. **2 substantive files:** `routes/garmin.py` (clusterer + `_coarse_sport`/`_sport_matches`/`_metric_within`/`_fingerprint_match` + constants + the one call site), `tests/test_garmin_bulk_source.py` (`TestCoarseSport` √ó4 + `TestClusterActivity` √ó8). **No DDL** (Slice 1 substrate already auto-applies) ‚Üí **no Neon apply owed**. **Tests:** full suite **3491 passed / 30 skipped**; **DESIGN ‚Äî #593 VOLUME/IN-TRANSIT EVENT WINDOWS + #592 RACE-LOCATION TERRAIN INFERENCE ‚Äî DESIGN SPECS WRITTEN (2026-06-21; branch `claude/issues-593-592-6llvfq`; PR opened + auto-merge armed on Andy's "open the pr and merge it").** Design-first session (no build), both specs in `designs/`. **#593 `Event_Windows_Slice6_VolumeWindows_Spec_v1.md`:** the deferred F9 `reduced_volume` flag ‚Üí two new `athlete_event_windows.override_type` values, `reduced_volume` + `no_training`, modeled as their own types that **union** with the feasibility overrides (Slice-1 overlap path). **Resolution model settled (Andy 2026-06-21, after two corrections):** NOT the reallocate‚Üíreformat‚Üídrop cascade my first draft proposed (Andy: that "introduces multiple new points of failure with the LLM looking for days or time slots it can't find") ‚Äî instead a **deterministic capacity reduction** feeding the existing grid. Per windowed week compute a capacity factor (`no_training` day = 0 + removed from the placement pool; `reduced_volume` day = the window's athlete-set `volume_pct`), scale the week's target hours by it, and call `session_grid._allocate_discipline` unchanged ‚Üí fewer/shorter sessions fall out of the existing hours‚Üícount math. **Session count ‚â§ available days by construction ‚Üí no off-limit slot for the LLM to fail to find** (the whole point). No trim-to-fit, no priority list, no volume conservation (a travel week is honestly lighter). The grid's existing phase logic protects key structure. **#592 `Race_Location_Terrain_Inference_Spec_v1.md` (Andy approved as-spec'd):** a new LLM terrain inference (Trigger #1 ‚Äî I/O contract spec'd, prompt body owed at build) that pre-fills the today-manual-only `_race_terrain_editor.html` as a reviewable suggestion (never auto-committed); weather **reuses** the existing `weather_client.get_expected_conditions` normals (no new weather inference); **no plan-gen change** ‚Äî 592 just populates `race_terrain`, which then flows the existing `race_terrain ‚Üí Layer 2B ‚Üí orchestrator` path. Carve is clean (a middle step between the race-logging UI and existing 2B consumption); crowd-sourced shared race-profile convergence noted as the future tie-in, not v1. **Andy decisions 2026-06-21 (folded into both specs): #593 `reduced_volume` = a per-window slider (`volume_pct` column, athlete-set, default ~0.5) ‚Äî NOT a fixed constant; #592 storage = persisted `race_terrain_suggested` column; #592 terrain breakdown = per-discipline (scoped per `discipline_id`, pct sums ~100 within each discipline).** **Remaining sign-off (at build only): Trigger #1 wording ‚Äî #593 overlay clause + #592 inference prompt body; #592 trigger timing (sync-at-save vs lazy-at-render).** **NEXT:** build each spec (one small slice apiece) when scheduled.

### Predecessor ‚Äî #424 v2 per-athlete load-progression grid

**LAYER 4 ‚Äî #424 v2 PER-ATHLETE LOAD-PROGRESSION GRID (3A coupling: trajectory / data-density / ACWR) ‚Äî BUILT (2026-06-20; branch `claude/issue-424-c9hum9`; PR pending Andy's go [PR-gated]).** Committed v2 follow-up to the #316 per-week volume-periodization grid (PR #422), which was **athlete-agnostic** (one fixed ramp/deload shape scaled only by the 2A bands). **Andy design-picks (AskUserQuestion √ó3): (1) scope = ramp steepness AND deeper deload when fatigued; (2) accept the proposed v1-default magnitudes; (3) `recent_trajectory.medium_term.direction` drives the ramp shape.** New `periodization.ramp_modulation_for(layer3a_payload) ‚Üí RampModulation(ramp_step_factor, deload_multiplier)` maps three 3A signals to the loading curve: **trajectory** (`building`‚Üí√ó1.15 steeper / `fatigued`¬∑`overreached`¬∑`detrained`‚Üí√ó0.85 gentler), **data_density** (`recent_workouts_count` <5‚Üí√ó0.80, <12‚Üí√ó0.90 ‚Äî sparse ‚Üí conservative, Spec ¬ß8.2 intent), **ACWR** (zone `non_functional_overreach`‚Üí√ó0.70 / `functional_overreach`‚Üí√ó0.85 cap; keyed on the 3A zone so the no-chronic-base sentinel caps correctly; never *accelerates* on ACWR alone), product clamped to [0.5,1.5]. The factor scales the **ramp STEP (slope)**, not absolute levels, so the Base/Build/Peak phase-mean renormalization keeps the **volume-neutral invariant for free** (a capped ramp just flattens the phase, never changes the total ‚Äî that stays the 2A allocation's job). Fatigue (`fatigued`/`overreached`/`detrained` OR `non_functional_overreach`) ALSO **deepens the deload** (`_M_DELOAD` 0.55 ‚àí0.075/signal, floor 0.40 = 60% cut, bottom of the cited 30‚Äì60% band); renormalization keeps it volume-neutral ‚Üí a sharper recovery dip, not a smaller phase. **Single chokepoint:** both consumers (validator band `validator.phase_week_volume_bands_hours`; prompt target `session_grid.build_session_grid` ‚Üê `per_phase._format_session_grid` ‚Üê `render_user_prompt`) route through `phase_week_multipliers_for_phase`, so threading `layer3a_payload` (already on `ctx.layer3a_payload` validator-side + a `render_user_prompt` param) into that one path keeps band + prompt automatically consistent. **Default `None` ‚Üí `NEUTRAL_MODULATION` ‚Üí the v1 athlete-agnostic curve** (graceful degradation; every existing test + payload-less entry point unchanged). Magnitudes are v1 defaults (`_K_*`/`_DELOAD_DEEPEN_STEP`), tune post-launch per Spec ¬ß8.3. **Rule #15:** `periodization.log_ramp_modulation` emits the per-athlete decision once per phase render (the pure `ramp_modulation_for` runs per memoized phase-week, so the log lives at the prompt-build path, not the hot fn). **No schema/contract/cache-revision change** (deterministic grid math; prompt *wording* unchanged ‚Üí no `LAYER4_PROMPT_REVISION` bump). Files: `layer4/periodization.py` (+modulation), `layer4/validator.py`, `layer4/session_grid.py`, `layer4/per_phase.py` (threading) + `tests/test_layer4_periodization.py` (+10 cases: per-signal mapping, clamp, volume-neutrality preserved under modulation, threading, defensive log). **Full suite 3050 passed / 30 skipped.** **LIVE-VERIFY owed (Andy-action ‚Äî container can't run plan-gen):** regen a plan for a `building` vs a `fatigued`/high-ACWR athlete ‚Üí `/admin/logs` shows the `ramp_modulation:` line + the loading weeks ramp steeper/flatter and the deload dips deeper respectively (green suite covers the math, not the live curve). **NEXT:** await Andy's "open the PR".

idempotent (only backfills active NULL rows; 3√ó apply = clean no-op, no UNIQUE collision); + a new `etl/layer0/validation/primary_movement_check.py` wired into `validate_layer0` (every active discipline must carry an `ENUM_MOVEMENTS` value ‚Äî fix-not-waive) so this regression can't silently recur. Old `etl/sources` migration **deleted** + de-referenced from `run_owed_layer0_migrations.sql` (now 3 includes). **Verified:** real-Postgres gate PASS end-to-end (all 10 checks incl. the new one; 24 active populated, 24 old rows kept as superseded history at `0A-v1.6.7`); full suite **2565 passed / 30 skipped**. **DONE ‚Äî applied to prod (Andy, 2026-06-15) + verified via the read-only diagnostics workflow: 24 active / 0 NULL / `0A-v1.6.8`;** the genesis **baseline was re-dumped to `etl/output/layer0_etl_v1.8.0.sql`** (PR [#626](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/626), gate-validated) so it no longer lags live.

### Predecessor ‚Äî WS-E2: deterministic strength-saturation cap

**WS-E2 ‚Äî deterministic strength-saturation cap (dose+2 + reallocate-with-variety) (2026-06-14, PR [#590](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/590), squash-merged to `main`, CI-green; closes WS-E2 [#584](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/issues/584); branch `claude/next-slice-implementation-37iur2`; handoff `handoffs/V5_Implementation_WSE2_StrengthSaturationCap_2026_06_14_Closing_Handoff_v1.md`; **north-star plan** `plans/Feasibility_Saturation_And_Locale_Retirement_Plan_v1.md` ¬ß7).** The ¬ß7 WS-E2 saturation backstop ‚Äî the last code workstream on the locale-retirement/feasibility-saturation plan. Andy picked it via `AskUserQuestion` and ratified the three design forks (Trigger #1/#5 stop-and-ask): **pre-synthesis grid pass**, **proportional-to-load_weight** reallocation, **build-now**. **Shipped:** new pure `session_grid.apply_strength_saturation_cap` runs **after** the ¬ß5.1.1 ceiling inside `build_session_grid` (gated on a new `strength_feasibility_tiers` kwarg ‚Äî bare callers omit it ‚Üí no cap, mirrors the `available_days`-gated ceiling). Weekly **failover** strength (terrain/craft-infeasible cardio composed as a strength substitution) is capped at `dose + 2` total ‚Äî a flat **+2 failover headroom every phase** (the prompt-added dose cancels out of the arithmetic). Over-cap excess is **trimmed lowest-priority-first** and **reallocated to feasible (exact/proxy/indoor) disciplines proportional to load_weight** (d'Hondt highest-averages), with a per-discipline absorption ceiling (a discipline can at most **double** in one pass) so volume spreads instead of dumping (Andy's "3 running + 3 cycling ‚Üí 6 running" failure mode). **Volume-conserving** ‚Äî sessions move strength‚Üífeasible 1:1, so the upstream session ceiling holds; excess no absorber can take **stays as strength** (training time preserved, never dropped ‚Äî E1/#579 still backstops the same-day collision crash). **T3 plan-refresh truncation fix ‚Äî size synthesis output budget to the session ceiling (2026-06-13, PR [#572](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/572))** (branch `claude/adoring-mccarthy-su0igw`, squash-merged to `main`; handoff `handoffs/V5_Implementation_T3RefreshOutputBudgetTruncationFix_2026_06_13_Closing_Handoff_v1.md`). **Ran the live T3 re-verify owed by #569 ‚Äî #569's `plan_start_date` fix is confirmed live (pv=67 cleared `_validate_inputs`), and the watch caught a *second* shipping bug.** pv=67 (`created_via=plan_refresh_t3`) reached real synthesis but failed `schema_violation ‚Ä¶ stop_reason=max_tokens, last_attempt_output_tokens=10000/ceiling=10000`: the refresh tiers carried flat output budgets that never absorbed the create path's per-session sizing, so a T3 cross-phase block (up to 56 sessions in one `record_refresh_sessions` call) truncated on a flat 10000 ceiling (~178 tok/session vs the create path's 1400). Because the truncation is a *retryable* `schema_violation`, pv=67 stayed `generating` and the every-minute cron deterministically re-drove it (advance lock 04:12‚Üí04:24) ‚Äî never `ready`. **Fix (Andy's call ‚Äî reuse the create-path balancing, not decomposition):** new `per_phase.block_output_budget(max_sessions, floor)` = `sessions √ó 1400 + 2000`, clamped to `_MODEL_MAX_OUTPUT_TOKENS=64000` (the `claude-sonnet-4-6` per-request output ceiling); the refresh driver `llm_layer4_plan_refresh` sizes `effective_max_tokens` to each tier's session ceiling via `_TIER_MAX_SESSIONS` (T1 7,600 / T2 21,600 / **T3 80,400‚Üí64,000 clamped**); T3 `DEFAULT_EXTENDED_THINKING_BUDGET` 6500‚Üí0 (under thinking the request is `max_tokens + thinking`, so a 64K output budget needs thinking off to stay under the model ceiling ‚Äî mirrors `per_phase`). The create per-phase block-mode now calls the same helper ‚Äî **behavior-preserving** (its per-week blocks are ‚â§21,600, clamp is a no-op). +4 tests; full suite **2366 passed / 30 skipped**; CI green. **Code-only, NO DDL.** **OWED ‚Äî live T3 re-verify (Andy's hands, post-#572):** re-run a T3 refresh on prod ‚Üí confirm the new pv reaches `ready` with a phase-correct `total_sessions` (diag token); #572 covers realistic ~20‚Äì35-session 4-week windows (‚âà28‚Äì49k, under 64K). **Two optional/contingent follow-ups filed** ([#574](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/issues/574) decompose T3 per-week ‚Äî the create machinery NOT ported, refresh is single-call; [#575](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/issues/575) per-pass give-up backstop so a retryable failure stops cron re-driving ‚Äî adjacent to #539), both `status:deferred`/`priority:low`, build only if their trigger fires. **NEXT:** unchanged ‚Äî the #541/#542/#543 plan-quality batch, then the compliance build-out (epics #353/#355/#356/#359).

### Predecessor ‚Äî Layer 0 slice 3b: per-table version resolution

`handoffs/V5_Implementation_Layer0_Slice3b_PerTableVersionResolution_2026_06_11_Closing_Handoff_v1.md` ‚Äî 2026-06-11 (**Layer 0 slice 3b ‚Äî per-table version resolution (epic [#488](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/issues/488)). Branch `claude/determined-dirac-5mjwge`; **PR [#544](https://github.com/ahorn885/exercise/pull/544)**. "Re-architect the lookup" (Andy's call) so a serving-relevant Layer 0 migration touches only the changed table, not the whole ~14-table family. **Finding that reshaped it:** every one of the 26 serving `etl_version` filters was already paired with `superseded_at IS NULL`, and supersede-before-insert keeps a table's active set single-version ‚Äî so the version predicate did ZERO row-selection work; its only live job was the cache key. **Decision (Trigger #3/#5, Andy signed off):** Option B / B2 / take-the-one-time-wipe ‚Äî **decouple serving from the version**. All 26 serving sites (5 Layer 2 builders + the 2 orchestrator `_q_` helpers) drop the `etl_version` predicate + bind and read `WHERE superseded_at IS NULL`; orphaned `version_0a/0b/0c` locals + helper params removed; builders still accept/validate/echo `etl_version_set` (cache provenance). `_q_current_etl_version_set` keeps the `{0A,0B,0C}` `dict[str,str]` contract but each value is now a per-table digest (`"sports=0A-v1.6.7;disciplines=0A-v1.6.8;‚Ä¶"`) from a single `UNION ALL` over the new `_LAYER0_TABLE_FAMILY` (24 tables, bucketed by table not prefix; per-table max). A serving-relevant migration bumps just the changed table ‚Üí digest shifts ‚Üí caches invalidate, no family re-stamp, no advance-the-max foot-gun. `terrain_gap_rules` (0C, created outside `schema.sql`, read by 2B) is mapped in; `supplement_vocabulary` stays out (own `supp_vocab.*` line). Drift guard `TestLayer0TableFamilyMap`. README shape-2 recipe + design ¬ß5.3 updated. **Suite 2294 / 30 skipped; etl/tests 185.** **OWED ‚Äî NO Neon migration this slice;** first prod deploy wipes plan caches once (auto, harmless) ‚Üí **cold-plan post-deploy verify** (terrain non-empty + real exercise pool; may also fix 2B terrain-gap proxies that were exact-matching the wrong `0C` version). **NEXT: phase 4** (design ¬ß6) ‚Äî freeze extractors + remaining workbooks, then DB‚Üíxlsx export.**)

Root-caused a latent Layer 4 error-handling gap, fixed it, then built the log-visibility surface the triage proved we needed.** The synthesizer over-emitted 3 sessions on one day; `Layer4Payload._check_two_per_day` rejected it (`max 2 sessions per day (got 3)`) ‚Äî but that pydantic `ValidationError` raised at `_build_payload_for_validation`, which sat **outside** the per-row parse `try/except` in `synthesize_phase`, so it escaped the typed-error contract ‚Üí the route catch-all discarded the WHOLE plan as "failed unexpectedly" over one bad block. Latent until #334 ran the first cold cone synthesizing fresh blocks (warm-cache pv=46 replayed cached blocks, never re-built a payload from a live fumble). **Fix:** wrap the payload construction, mirroring the parse step ‚Äî a `ValidationError` now retries in-loop and, after `capped_retries`, raises `Layer4OutputError('schema_violation')` (a `_RETRYABLE_BLOCK_CODES` member), so the block re-synthesizes instead of killing the plan; covers every top-level invariant uniformly. **Log-visibility (Rule #14, option 1):** the triage was blind because the Vercel runtime-log MCP truncates/groups and the admin inspect page is login-walled ‚Äî so the real fault was unreadable until Andy hand-pasted the traceback. Shipped a durable `plan_versions.generation_traceback` (best-effort persist in `_mark_plan_failed`) + a token-gated `GET /admin/plan/<id>/diag` JSON endpoint readable past the login wall (admin session OR constant-time `DIAG_TOKEN`). **CLAUDE.md Rule #14** codifies the lesson: ask for the log, don't infer around an unreadable one. Suite **1855/16**. **Migration owed + DONE this session (Andy):** `generation_traceback` column applied on Neon; `DIAG_TOKEN` set in Vercel + shared. **Follow-ups: #350** (log-drain hard-kill backstop), **#351** (per-day clamp so the >2/day fumble self-heals without a retry). **Next: re-run the PGE e2e** (now both reach-race-day + resilience are live) and read the result from the diag endpoint ‚Üí the ¬ß14 within-phase coherence read (still owed) ‚Üí remaining #333 sub-items.

### Predecessor ‚Äî #334 fixed: event-mode plans reach race day with a 2-week terminal Taper

**Closed the #334 go-live blocker: event-mode plans were stopping ~1 week short of race day and dropping the Taper.** Two compounding bugs: (1) 3B `_time_to_event_weeks` floored (`days // 7`) ‚Üí a 48-day gap resolved to 6 weeks not 7, dropping the final partial week; (2) `_allocate_weeks_standard`'s `int()` truncation floored a sub-1-week Taper to 0 ‚Üí it was dropped ‚Üí `scope_end_date` landed on Peak's end (which *also* silently kills the Decision-4 race-week brief + Taper `coaching_flags`, both of which only attach to an existing Taper). **Fix (spec-first, two amendments then code):** 3B horizon ‚Üí race-day-inclusive `ceil((days + 1) / 7)` (the `+1` counts race day so an exact-multiple gap doesn't end a day short; PGE 48-day gap ‚Üí 7 weeks, ends exactly on race day); Layer 4 event-mode terminal phase floored at **2 weeks** (taper wk + race wk; race week stays the final Taper week, no 5th phase), shortfall reclaimed one week at a time from a non-terminal phase (Base first, else largest) without starving any phase below 1 week. **Safety insulation:** the DNF-recurrence HITL trigger (`weeks < window`) was switched to a local conservative **floor** so the new ceil can't inflate the count past the window boundary and suppress a warning that should fire (a 77-day gap is genuinely inside the 12-week `quad_failure` window). PR split to its own #346 (off main); #345 restored to #333-only + merged. **Known residual ‚Üí #347:** whole-week structure + no `event_date` clamp can overshoot race day by ‚â§6 days when race day falls mid-week (exact/no-impact for PGE); trimming needs a session-level clamp. Suite **1851/16**; **no migration**. **Cache note:** the changed `time_to_event_weeks` makes the first post-deploy event-mode gen a cold cone (expected). **Next: re-run the PGE e2e (fresh `pv`)** to confirm the plan spans through 2026-07-17 with a 2-week Taper, then the ¬ß14 within-phase coherence read (still owed) ‚Üí remaining #333 sub-items.

### Predecessor ‚Äî plan-gen six-link failure chain: diagnose‚Üídecompose‚Üítimeout‚Üírebind (pv=41‚Üí45)

THIS is why #327's bump "did nothing" (it sized block mode only) and why runs differed (whether a seam fires is stochastic). Andy's "a token bump can't be the cure" was right. **(3) #330 (D-77 Slice 3)** ‚Äî decompose seam re-synth into resumable, cache-wired, budget-gated **week-blocks** (21,600 ceiling + seam constraints; disjoint `phase_idx` band `[500,1000)` so the stall counter sees them as progress ‚Äî no route SQL). **(4) #331** ‚Äî pv=43/44's untyped `ValueError: Streaming is required`: the Anthropic SDK refuses a non-streaming call when `max_tokens > 21,333`, and the thinking attempt sends `21,600+5,000=26,600`; a **latent landmine** #330 was first to cross. Fix: pin an explicit `timeout` (client + per-request) ‚Äî disables the guard for every caller. **(5) #332** ‚Äî pv=45 synthesized 5 blocks + ran the seam re-synth clean through Build w1‚Äìw4 (real coherent programming), then crashed at **persist** on a `UniqueViolation` (a pv=39-stamped session in pv=45's plan): the per-block cache is shared across plan versions but the per-block hydrate path never rebound `plan_version_id` like the ¬ß9.4 whole-payload path does. Fix: rebind on hydrate (self-heals the poisoned cache on next read) + force the payload's id at persist (safety net). Suite **1845/16**; no migration. [**Superseded next-move:** "merge #332 + proof run" ‚Äî done as pv=46 (above), which reached `ready` and closed #324.]

### Predecessor ‚Äî plan-gen poller 500 regression fix (PR #312)

`handoffs/V5_Implementation_PlanGen_D77_PollerGeneratingMapping_504GiveUpFix_2026_05_29_Closing_Handoff_v1.md` ‚Äî 2026-05-29 (**plan-gen poller 500 regression fix ‚Äî PR #311's two new `'generating'` outcomes were never mapped in the poller route, so every multi-block plan KeyError-500'd to "taking longer than expected"; branch `claude/ecstatic-hamilton-NoWBX`, PR #312**)

**Fixed the regression PR #311 introduced into plan-gen.** PR #311's concurrency guard + per-invocation budget added two `{"status": "generating", ...}` returns to `_advance_plan_generation`, but the poller route `generate_plan` was never taught to handle them ‚Äî it fell through to `jsonify({"status": "failed", "error": outcome['error']})`, KeyError-ing on the missing `'error'` key ‚Üí **HTTP 500 on every intermediate poll**. The budget makes `budget_partial_progress` the *normal* path for any plan needing >1 pass, so essentially every real multi-block plan 500'd its way to the client's give-up message ("This is taking longer than expected. Please try again.") even though the cone was healthy and caching blocks. Fix: (1) `generate_plan` now maps `'generating'` ‚Üí `{"status":"generating"}` (keep-polling); (2) `templates/plan_create/progress.html` replaces the *total*-poll cap (`MAX_ATTEMPTS=20`, far too few now each pass does ~1 week-block) with a *consecutive-transport-failure* cap ‚Äî a clean response resets it; the server-side 900s wall-clock stall backstop remains the real terminal guard. 2 code/template files + `tests/test_routes_plan_create.py` (+5 `TestGeneratePlanRoute`); 50 passed in that file, 160 combined. **No migration.** **This unblocks the still-owed D-77 convergence re-run** ‚Äî that gating proof (CARRY_FORWARD owed #1) could never have gone green at the client before, because the poller 500'd on every budget-partial pass. The live code state otherwise matches the predecessor below (D-77 convergence, PR #294/#311, re-run owed).

### Predecessor ‚Äî D-77 Layer 2E cache-key determinism + stall-backstop orphan-scoping (full record in `handoffs/`)

`handoffs/V5_Implementation_PlanGen_D77_Layer2ECacheKeyDeterminism_StallBackstopOrphanScoping_2026_05_27_Closing_Handoff_v1.md` ‚Äî 2026-05-27 (**D-77 non-convergence REAL ROOT CAUSE found in the prod logs + fixed ‚Äî Layer 2E `computed_at` cache-key non-determinism (PR #199, merged `9012430`) + stall-backstop orphan-scoping (PR #200); branch `claude/review-run-logs-A4JVs`**)

**Finally read the prod Vercel logs (prior 3 sessions diagnosed code-only) and pinned the actual non-convergence root cause ‚Äî a SECOND instance of the c4f9160 cache-key non-determinism bug that fix missed.** The two failed `plan_version_id=29` runs 504-looped with `max_tokens=9200` live + `schema_violation` GONE (PR #197 worked) but `accepted=True` never appearing. **Bug A (PR #199, merged):** `Layer2EPayload.computed_at` (`layer2e/builder.py:1156`) was stamped full-microsecond `datetime.now()`; the cone rebuilds every resumable pass, and `computed_at` folds into `layer2e_hash` ‚Üí `plan_create_key` ‚Üí EVERY `compute_block_cache_key`, so each pass minted different block keys ‚Üí every cached block orphaned ‚Üí re-synthesized from scratch each pass ‚Üí 504-loop re-burning the full extended-thinking synthesis each minute (the ~$50). Same class as c4f9160 (which day-anchored `layer1.as_of` + `layer2a.generated_at`) but it missed 2E (2E runs after 3B, so it poisons Layer 4 keys but not 3A/3B ‚Äî which is why 3A/3B cached fine and only Layer 4 looped). Fix: day-anchor `computed_at` to the cone's logical `today`. Plus diagnostics: `cached_wrappers.py` logs `call_cache_key` + each component layer-hash per pass (key drift ‚Üí names the guilty layer in one read); `cache.py` logs per-block cache HIT/MISS. **Bug B (PR #200):** after PR #199 deployed, new plans `pv=30..33` failed IMMEDIATELY ‚Äî the D-77 stall backstop false-tripped because `_generation_stalled` measured `NOW() - MAX(block.created_at)` scoped to the USER, and `pv=29`'s orphaned rows (>1h old) anchored the 900s window in the past. Fix: bound `_generation_stalled` + `_count_cached_blocks` to `created_at >= pv.created_at` (per-plan progress only). 2 code + 2 test files across the two PRs + `Layer4_Spec ¬ß11.5`. Suite **1796 passed / 16 skipped**. **No migration** (query/sampling-level; existing orphan rows just stop mattering). **‚öÝ Owed (Andy's hands): merge PR #200 + redeploy, then create ONE fresh plan** ‚Äî it should now get past the gate (Bug B) and CONVERGE (Bug A). Proof in the new logs: `call_cache_key=<X>` IDENTICAL across passes (was drifting); per-block `HIT` on later passes; `<phase>:w<n> done ‚Äî ‚Ä¶ accepted=True`; plan reaches `ready`. Residual watch (Trigger #5, data-gated): if the per-attempt `llm call <N>ms ‚Ä¶ max_tokens=9200` line shows a single dense-week call near 300s, shrink the block / trim thinking budget. ### Predecessor ‚Äî D-77 block-mode `max_tokens` truncation fix (full record in `handoffs/`)

`handoffs/V5_Implementation_PlanGen_D77_BlockMaxTokens_SchemaViolationFix_2026_05_27_Closing_Handoff_v1.md` ‚Äî 2026-05-27 (**D-77 block-mode `max_tokens` truncation fix ‚Äî the cone/truncation watch-item fired; branch `claude/plan-gen-schema-violation-tpu23`**)

**The cone/truncation fix (PR #195) worked ‚Äî the re-run no longer 504-looped, but failed with a bounded `schema_violation` ("Plan synthesis failed (schema_violation). Adjust your inputs and try again."), exactly the predecessor's ¬ß6/¬ß11.5 watch-item.** The per-block budget guard + empty-tool escalation stopped the loop, but the **forced-tool retry runs with thinking OFF**, so `max_tokens` is the *entire* output budget (no `+ thinking_budget` headroom). The per-phase default `max_tokens=4000` predates the dense `PlanSession` schema (per-session `cardio_blocks` + `strength_exercises` + 240-char notes ‚âà 400‚Äì600 output tokens), so a full high-frequency week (up to 14 sessions, the PGE 6-discipline norm) truncated mid-`sessions` ‚Üí incomplete tool call ‚Üí `schema_violation`. **Fix:** block mode (`week_range` set) now sizes the output budget to the unit's session ceiling ‚Äî `effective_max_tokens = max(max_tokens, max_sessions_this_unit √ó _BLOCK_OUTPUT_TOKENS_PER_SESSION(600) + _BLOCK_OUTPUT_TOKENS_OVERHEAD(800))` = **9200** for a 1-week block; never below the caller's value. Higher `max_tokens` is only a ceiling (billed/latency cost tracks emitted tokens; the `_PER_BLOCK_BUDGET_MS=120_000` guard still bounds time) and it also gives the *first* thinking attempt more post-thinking output room. Whole-phase seam-resynth (`week_range=None`, ‚â§56 sessions) is intentionally NOT scaled ‚Äî that's the Slice-3 stitcher's path, not a token bump. 1 code file (`layer4/per_phase.py`) + 2 tests (`TestBlockOutputBudget`) + `Layer4_Spec ¬ß11.5` in place. Suite **1795 passed / 16 skipped** (+2). **No migration** (`max_tokens` is a sampling param, not in any cache key/schema). **‚öÝ Owed (Andy's hands): redeploy (merge) + re-run the PGE plan.** **NOTE: diagnosis is code-evidence-based ‚Äî the prod log was not in hand this session** (Andy pasted only the athlete message). The re-run proof is the per-attempt log line `synthesize_phase: <phase>:w<n> ‚Ä¶ out=N max_tokens=9200` (`out` should land BELOW the ceiling, not pin it) + the `<phase>:w<n> done ‚Äî ‚Ä¶ accepted=True` summary firing. If a `schema_violation` still surfaces, send back that line + the route's `_advance_plan_generation: Layer4 ‚Ä¶ (schema_violation) ‚Ä¶ : <detail>` (`detail` carries `stop_reason` + cause) ‚Äî `stop_reason=max_tokens` near 9200 ‚áí raise further / trim thinking budget; anything else ‚áí a different fix. Coherence (design ¬ß14) still UNVERIFIED until a plan reaches `ready`.

### Predecessor ‚Äî D-77 cone cache-key determinism + synthesizer truncation + per-block budget (full record in `handoffs/`)

`handoffs/V5_Implementation_PlanGen_D77_ConeCacheKeyDeterminism_SynthTruncationFix_2026_05_27_Closing_Handoff_v1.md` ‚Äî 2026-05-27 (**D-77 non-convergence ROOT CAUSE fixed ‚Äî cone cache-key determinism + synthesizer truncation + per-block budget; branch `claude/plan-gen-timeout-logs-caH8Q`**)

**The instrumented re-run (`plan_version_id=27`) pinned the stall to TWO independent bugs; fixed both.** (1) **Cone cache keys were non-deterministic across function invocations** ‚Äî `Layer1Payload.as_of` + `Layer2APayload.rationale_metadata.generated_at` were stamped with full-precision `datetime.utcnow()` and hashed into `layer1_hash`/`layer2a_hash`, which fold into EVERY Layer 4 cache key (3A/3B/`compute_block_cache_key`/refresh/single-session/brief). So 3A + 3B re-ran cold on **every** resumable pass (prod logs: the live-run `Layer3A/3BEvidenceBasisWarning` in 17/17 passes, ~150s/pass) and any synthesized block was orphaned next pass ‚Äî D-77 monotonic convergence was **structurally impossible**, which is why decomposition never helped (this overturns the predecessor's "warm 3A/3B cone" assumption ‚Äî it had no per-layer cache instrumentation). Fix: day-anchor both timestamps (matches the 3A `as_of` day-granular cache semantics; neither field is consumed ‚Äî pure provenance). (2) **The synthesizer starved its own output on the thinking budget** ‚Äî `attempt 1/3 llm call 142528ms (in=6896 out=9000)` then `tool_args keys=[]`: under thinking the ceiling is `max_tokens(4000)+budget(5000)=9000`, the model spent it all thinking and emitted a contentless tool call ‚Üí no sessions ‚Üí never cached. Fix: `invoke_tool_call` treats an empty tool call like a missing block ‚Üí fires the existing forced-tool retry (thinking off ‚Üí full output budget, can't decline). Plus a structural **per-block budget** (`_PER_BLOCK_BUDGET_MS=120_000`) in `synthesize_phase`: once a block spends its LLM-time budget it won't start another attempt ‚Äî accepts best-effort (caches ‚Üí progress) or fails terminally fast (`synthesis_budget_exhausted`), never 504-loops. 4 code files (`layer1/builder.py`, `layer2a/builder.py`, `llm_invocation.py`, `layer4/per_phase.py`) + 13 tests (escalation √ó10, hash-determinism √ó2, budget-guard √ó1) + `Layer4_Spec ¬ß11.5` updated in place. Suite **1793 passed / 16 skipped** (+13). **No migration.** **‚öÝ Owed (Andy's hands): redeploy (merge), then re-run the PGE plan** ‚Äî expect it to CONVERGE now (3A/3B cache after pass 1 ‚Üí blocks cache ‚Üí `ready`). Watch the Vercel log: `synthesize_phase: <phase>:w<n> done ‚Äî ‚Ä¶` should fire (it never has), and the cone should NOT re-run 3A/3B every pass. If the forced-tool retry still truncates a dense ~14-session week against `max_tokens=4000`, the follow-on is bumping block-mode `max_tokens` (the budget guard keeps it failing fast, not looping, meanwhile).

### Predecessor ‚Äî D-77 per-block budget instrumentation (full record in `handoffs/`)

`handoffs/V5_Implementation_PlanGen_D77_PerBlockBudget_Instrumentation_2026_05_27_Closing_Handoff_v1.md` ‚Äî 2026-05-27 (**D-77 per-block synthesis-budget finding + diagnostic instrumentation; branch `claude/plan-generation-timeout-8s1Hn`**)

**Found why the re-run STILL stalled, then shipped logging-only instrumentation (Andy's gate: "add logging first").** Andy re-ran the coherence walk on the deployed wall-clock-backstop fix (#189, now under prod #190) and got the same "Plan generation stalled." The prod runtime log for `plan_version_id=25` shows: 3A/3B were warm cache hits (cone NOT the bottleneck), week-1 block synthesis was reached immediately, then **every** generate pass (poller + cron) 504'd with an `api.anthropic.com` call in flight, and the wall-clock backstop tripped at ~960s with **zero blocks cached**. **Root cause:** a single week-block's `synthesize_phase` retry loop (up to `capped_retries+1`=3 extended-thinking calls, √óa forced-tool fallback) is **in-memory / not resumable across function invocations**, and the block caches only after the loop returns ‚Äî so a block that needs retries exceeds the immovable 300s cap, 504-kills mid-loop, caches nothing, and restarts from attempt 1 next pass: an infinite loop, the SAME failure as the original `plan_version_id=23` incident. D-77 Slice 1 shrank the *cache unit* (phase‚Üíweek) but never bounded a single block's *synthesis cost*. The backstop is healthy; the unit still doesn't fit. At an `AskUserQuestion` gate Andy chose **"add logging first"** over committing to a fix ‚Äî so this session is **instrumentation only, no behavior change**: `layer4/per_phase.py` now logs per-attempt LLM latency + the previously-silent per-block validator-rejection rule set (+ parse / no-`sessions` detail + a per-block summary) under a greppable `<phase>:w<week>` tag. `Layer4_Spec ¬ß11.5` records the open limitation. Suite **1780 passed / 16 skipped** (unchanged ‚Äî pure `print`). **No migration. ‚öÝ Owed (Andy's hands): redeploy (merge), re-run the PGE plan (it will likely stall again ‚Äî that's expected; the goal is the logs), then send back the `synthesize_phase:` log lines** so next session reads *why* blocks retry and picks the bounding fix (candidates: per-block wall-clock budget ‚Üí best-effort; lower retry/thinking budget; finer decomposition ‚Äî all Trigger #5).

### Predecessor ‚Äî D-77 Slice 2 backstop fix (full record in `handoffs/`)

**Fixed the Slice 2 progress backstop, which was false-failing plans ~46s in.** The first real-LLM coherence walk (`plan_version_id=24`) hit "Plan generation stalled," but the Vercel log showed a single in-flight Anthropic call and **no `schema_violation`** ‚Äî so the Slice 2 backstop was strangling the run, NOT the decomposition. Fix: a **wall-clock gate** (`_generation_stalled`, `_STALL_WALLCLOCK_S=900`) ‚Äî trip only when no block has cached for ~3 function budgets, measured on the DB clock (`NOW()` vs. the newest block's `created_at`, else generation start); robust to a 504-killed pass and to concurrent cron/poller calls.
